Please continue.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: For those of you who haven't met me. I'm Emily Cooper, and I’m so excited to be in Paris. I'm looking forward to getting to know each and every one of you and, likewise, having you get to know me. Your name, monsieur?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">L</strong>: My name is Luc.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: Yes, Luc?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">L</strong>: Why are you shouting?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: Sorry. Your company works with some of the biggest brands in the luxury sector, from Chanel to YSL. And that makes Savoir, your company, or, if I may be so bold, our company, a brand in itself. But to build a brand, you must create meaningful social media engagement. May I ask who's responsible for your social media here?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">M</strong>: Patricia.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: Make sense. Anyway, it's not just about the number of followers, It's about content, trust,  interest, and engagement.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">L</strong>: Excuse me, but the French are masters of social media.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: True. But Americans intented it, which is why I hope to become a valuable member of your team by adding an American point of view to your fabulous French clients.</p></section></section><section 94);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链解析</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(239, 237, 222);padding: 25px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(94, 127, 94);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在Emily开始自我介绍之前，说到自己在用自学软件学习法语，可是还没有学会时，用到了”kick in“这个表达。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：I did Rosetta Stone on the plane, but<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> it hasn't kicked in yet</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说到"kick in"大家想到的画面可能是这样子的。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 80%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5604167" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/L4LJPfaSIKe2ZYbG6icITicznH6BG1kEibTP2kialicQD46J5pz1eQe2O2TD0ficODPicOFx9MhicHia5YukNibtmyWwBd9Q/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="480" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(94, 127, 94);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">然而，"kick in"本意是“开始生效”的意思，在这里Emily说自学软件还没有起效，引</span><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">申意思就是自己还不会说法语。我们来看几个例句，加深一下对这个词链的理解。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：When are these drugs going to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick in</strong>? </span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这药什么时候才会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">起作用</strong>？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：There is not much <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick in</strong> the cocktail.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这种鸡尾酒没有多少<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">劲儿</strong>。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3</strong>：That pill I took really <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kicked in</strong> fast.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>安眠药真是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">见效</strong>快。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;padding: 0px 10px;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"># kick up your heels 轻轻松松 #</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(94, 127, 94);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家大概都看到过一匹年轻的俊马在宽阔的草原上兴高彩烈地奔跑的情景吧！这是一幅很美丽的图象，马的前腿往前伸展，后腿很有节奏地往上踢。这个俗语就是建筑在这一形像之上的。To kick up one's heels，从字面上来解释就是：把后脚往上踢。但是，实际上to kick up one's heels是用来形容人们到外面去寻欢作乐，就像马在草原上奔跑一样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I can't find any point in losing time on those shit. Why don't we just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick up our heels</strong>. 我找不到任何在这些烂事情上浪费时间的意义。我们为何不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">轻松一下</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section 94);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链解析</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(239, 237, 222);padding: 25px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(94, 127, 94);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在Emily开始自我介绍之前，说到自己在用自学软件学习法语，可是还没有学会时，用到了”kick in“这个表达。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：I did Rosetta Stone on the plane, but<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> it hasn't kicked in yet</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说到"kick in"大家想到的画面可能是这样子的。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 80%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5604167" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/L4LJPfaSIKe2ZYbG6icITicznH6BG1kEibTP2kialicQD46J5pz1eQe2O2TD0ficODPicOFx9MhicHia5YukNibtmyWwBd9Q/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="480" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(94, 127, 94);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 13px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">然而，"kick in"本意是“开始生效”的意思，在这里Emily说自学软件还没有起效，引</span><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">申意思就是自己还不会说法语。我们来看几个例句，加深一下对这个词链的理解。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：When are these drugs going to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick in</strong>? </span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这药什么时候才会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">起作用</strong>？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：There is not much <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick in</strong> the cocktail.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这种鸡尾酒没有多少<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">劲儿</strong>。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3</strong>：That pill I took really <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kicked in</strong> fast.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>安眠药真是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">见效</strong>快。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section be<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> kick -ass</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我预言今年一定<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">很棒</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 30px 0% 10px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;background-color: rgb(124, 149, 124);min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;padding: 0px 10px;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"># kick up your heels 轻轻松松 #</p></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(94, 127, 94);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家大概都看到过一匹年轻的俊马在宽阔的草原上兴高彩烈地奔跑的情景吧！这是一幅很美丽的图象，马的前腿往前伸展，后腿很有节奏地往上踢。这个俗语就是建筑在这一形像之上的。To kick up one's heels，从字面上来解释就是：把后脚往上踢。但是，实际上to kick up one's heels是用来形容人们到外面去寻欢作乐，就像马在草原上奔跑一样。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I can't find any point in losing time on those shit. Why don't we just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">kick up our heels</strong>. 我找不到任何在这些烂事情上浪费时间的意义。我们为何不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">轻松一下</strong>。</p></section><section </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">invitation   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE /ˌɪnvɪˈteɪʃn/  NAmE /ˌɪnvɪˈteɪʃn/    n.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">[countable] a spoken or written request to sb to do sth or to go somewhere </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（口头或书面的）邀请</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to issue  / extend an invitation</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">发出／致送邀请</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to accept  / turn down  / decline an invitation</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接受／拒绝／婉拒邀请</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pretend </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE /prɪˈtend/    NAmE /prɪˈtend/  v.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">[intransitive, transitive] to behave in a particular way, in order to make other people believe sth that is not true 假装；佯装</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’m tired of having to pretend all the time.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我讨厌老得装假。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pretend (to sb) (that…)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He pretended to his family that everything was fine.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他对家人佯称一切都好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We pretended (that) nothing had happened.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们假装什么事情也没发生。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pretend to do sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He pretended not to notice.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他假装没注意。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She didn’t love him, though she pretended to.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她并不爱他，虽然她装出爱的样子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pretend sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(formal) She pretended an interest she did not feel.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她毫无兴趣却装作有兴趣。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">misunderstand   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE /mɪsʌndə’stænd     NAmE /mɪsʌndər’stænd/  v.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to fail to understand someone or something correctly 误解，误会</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don’t misunderstand me. She’s a very nice person when you get to know her.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不要误解我的意思。你了解她后就会知道她是个很好的人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> Sallie</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">没有别的衣服？萨丽说，这太有意思了</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">—</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Caspian nodded to Bern and then stood aside. Bern and Drinian took a step forward and each seized one end of the table. They lifted it, and flung it on one side of the hall where it rolled over, scattering a cascade of letters, dossiers, ink-pots, pens, sealing-wax and documents. Then, not roughly but as firmly as if their hands were pincers of steel, they plucked Gumpas out of his chair and deposited him, facing it, about four feet away. Caspian at once sat down in the chair and laid his naked sword across his knees.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">凯斯宾对伯恩点点头就站到一边。伯恩和德里宁上前一步，各自抓住桌子一头。他们抬起桌子一扔，桌子就滚到大厅一边了，把信件、档案、墨水缸、笔、封口蜡和公文撒得一地。于是，他们伸出手去，虽然动作不粗野，缺牢如钢钳，一把将冈帕斯从椅子里揪出来，把他揪到椅子前四英尺开外的地方。凯斯宾马上在椅子里坐下，把出鞘的剑横搁在双膝上。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你们产品的批发价是多少?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我们几个批发商的情况都不一样，所以本会计年度的费用支出不好确定。但差别很小，大约上下浮动0.2%。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那多少会影响到你们的底线吧?毕竟你们的定价相当固定。那你们产品的零售价是多少?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 零售价是每套29.95美元，定价时我们把供货成本的变化因素考虑进去了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 包括税吗?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不包括，这是税前价。不同的销售区税率各不相同，所以我们很难把它核算进去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那么你们的利润率是多少?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我们的利润率大约在20%左右。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How much do you pay wholesale for your products?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: We have a few different wholesale vendors, so our cost varies a bit over the fiscal year. But the difference is miniscule, a fluctuation of about 0.2%.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: That must impact your bottom line at least a little bit, doesn't it? After all, your sticker price is pretty much set in stone. How much do they go for retail?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Retail price is 29.95 per unit. We take into consideration changes in supply cost when figuring this price.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Is that including tax?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, that's the price before tax. The tax rate is varies from different marketing areas, so it is difficult for us to figure in.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：How much is your profit margin then?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Our profit margin is in the neighborhood of 20%.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’ve now got the hang of learning English verbs.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我已经找到学习英语动词的_________了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">窍门</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">7.2 早读原文</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: class="rich_pages js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.31640625" data-s="300,640" style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. steal /stiːl/ 包含难发音组/iːl/；先练习/<strong style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);font-size: 14px;text-align: left;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">iː</strong>/的发音：</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><img class="rich_pages js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.25937183383991896" data-s="300,640" 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. the best of all ways 一切办法中最好的办法</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：the best of all...  最好的...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They're all good players, but she's<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> the best of all</strong></em></span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们都是优秀运动员，而她更是其中的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">佼佼者</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. lengthen v.(使)延长，(使)加长 = get longer</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">length + en= lengthen ; -en后缀，表动词“使变得...”</strong></p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: disc;box-sizing: border-box;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">widen  (使)变宽</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">shorten（使）变短，缩短</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">strengthen （使）变强；加强</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">weaken (使)变弱；削弱</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...</p></li></ul><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I need to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lengthen </strong></em></span>this skirt.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我需要把这条裙子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">放长</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The days <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lengthen </strong></em></span>in spring.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">春天白昼会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">变长</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I will <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lengthen </strong></em></span>your life by not telling my husband.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 你还能活的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">长久些</strong>，等我丈夫回来时。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: </strong></em></span>data <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">from </strong></em></span>a <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">from </strong></em></span>mom's purse.</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">TeacherGwen</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px dotted rgb(197, 227, 211);padding-top: 3px;width: 100%;margin-bottom: -3px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="height: 5px;line-height: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 5px;height: 5px;float: left;border-radius: 50%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(197, 227, 211);box-sizing: border-box;"></span> <span style="width: 5px;height: 5px;float: left;border-radius: 50%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(197, 227, 211);margin-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"></span> <span style="width: 5px;height: 5px;float: left;border-radius: 50%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(197, 227, 211);margin-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"></span> <span style="width: 5px;height: 5px;float: left;border-radius: 50%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(197, 227, 211);margin-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"></span> <span style="width: 5px;height: 5px;float: left;border-radius: 50%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(197, 227, 211);margin-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"></span> </section><section style="clear: both;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">早读|<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">口语</strong></span>|阅读|翻译|听写</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">等你好久了，点击关注我们</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">了解更多口语表达~~</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">排版|编辑 Angelia</span></p></section></section></section></section></section></sectio</section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.please</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 使高兴；讨好</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：More than anything, I want to please you.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最重要的是，我想让你高兴。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.kind offer </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好意</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：I appreciate your kind offer but cannot accept it.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你的好意我心领了，但是不能接受。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.curl英 /kɜːl/ 美 /kɝl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 使…卷曲；使卷起来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 卷曲；盘绕</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 卷曲；卷发；螺旋状物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：She had curled her hair for the event.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她为这次活动卷了头发。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.redden英 /'redn/ 美 /' redn /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. （使）变红；（人）脸红，害羞；（眼睛）哭红</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：He could feel his face reddening with embarrassment.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他能感到自己因为尴尬而脸红了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.earring英 /'ɪərɪŋ/ 美 /'ɪrɪŋ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 耳环，耳饰</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">wear earrings 戴耳环</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">wear a necklace 戴项链</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.stare英 /steə/ 美 /stɛr/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 凝视，盯着看；显眼</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 凝视，盯着看</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 凝视；注视</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">stare at 凝视，盯住</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">stare into 凝视</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：The girl stared at him in disbelief, shaking her head.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">女孩摇着头，不相信地盯着他看。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">表示“看”的单词和短语：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1、look</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">look at 意思是看着，强调的是“看”这个动作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I didn't dare look at him.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不敢看他。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2、see</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">see的含义是”看到“，强调的是看到的结果，也就是说看到了什么</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Did you see what happened？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你看见出什么事了吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">see还有看望的意思，例如：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Kids are so happy to see their grandpa in the old village.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孩子们非常开心去那个老村子里看望他们的爷爷。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3、watch</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">watch的意思是看一个具体的东西，如电影，电视等，强调欣赏的概念。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Children are told not to watch too much TV, but we know anything can't stop them watching TV.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">都在说别给小孩子看太多电视，但是我们知道似乎没什么能阻止他们看电视。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4、read</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">read主要用于看书、看报、看资料等，强调看的内容的详细特性。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He's read many books since he join the READING CLUB.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">加入阅读俱乐部以来，他已经看了大量的书。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5、glance at</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">glance at 意思是瞥了一眼。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She noticed that someone in the corner was glancing at her.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她留意到角落里有人瞥了她一眼。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6、glare at</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">glare at意思是生气地看着，怒视着。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His father glared at him for his bad performance in the exam.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">知道他考砸了，他爸生气地看着他。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7、stare at</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">stare at意思是盯着看</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She stares at her friend and laughs.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她盯着她的朋友，大笑起来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center center;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcaNicK4nbQaWlHrqBKiaAQ4GoErHrrfWJ5uvdUI6xtMnoxJfmtXBcUyoNSicszDSLuRoDNTKFYibjyFg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="200" style="width: 0.5em;border-top-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Friday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">“I have a pretty blue dress I can</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">’t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> wear any more, Meg”, said Belle</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">我有一件很漂亮的蓝裙子，我穿不下了，麦格，贝拉说，</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">“I</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> will please me if you wea</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">r i</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">t”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">你如果穿上它我会很高兴。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 40);box-sizing: border-box;">穿上吧，贝拉说。你穿上会非常漂亮的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: lady</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: party</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">At first, she fel</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span><span 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">可不久她发现那些平常不注意她的人开始跟她攀谈了。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 40);box-sizing: border-box;">几个年轻人原先只盯着她看，现在都希望被介绍给她。</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Two merchants of Calormen at once approached. The Calormen have dark faces and long beards. They wear flowing robes and orange-coloured turbans, and they are a wise, wealthy, courteous, cruel and ancient people. They bowed most politely to Caspian and paid him long compliments, all about the fountains of prosperity irrigating the gardens of prudence and virtue - and things like that - but of course what they wanted was the money they had paid.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">两个卡乐门商人立刻上前。卡乐门人长着黑脸膛，留着长胡子。他们穿着飘拂的长袍，扎着橙红色头巾，他们是聪明、富裕、谦恭而残忍的古老民族。他们极其恭敬地向凯斯宾鞠躬，对他说了长长一篇恭维话，说的全是什么繁荣昌盛的源泉灌溉贤明和德行的花园——还有类似的话——不过他们的目的当然是想收回付出的那笔钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">F: 你不是打算下周给我们开个培训会吗?你的陈述报告准备得怎么样了?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: 我很难把培训的题目缩小。我想讲讲如何提高我们的销售技巧,可是要说的话太多,很难组织。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">F: 我们的培训团体不会太大，所以你有更多的时间兼顾更多的方面。如果大家都积极参与并注意听讲的话，我们可以在一个半小时的时间内涉及很多方面。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: 我想重点对打推销电话提一些建议，而且我也希望再增加一些角色扮演活动，这样大家能把我要讲的内容实际应用一下。你认为大家会喜欢角色扮演吗?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">F: 我想有些人可能会觉得在全班同学面前做角色扮演有点害羞……不过你对自己的话题很有热情的话，你可以帮助大家放松情绪并愿意尝试下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">F: Aren't you going to give us a training workshop next week? How are things going on your preparation for the presentation?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: I'm having trouble narrowing down my topic for the training. I want to speak about how to improve our sales technique, but there is so much to say, it's hard to get organized.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">F: Our training group won't be very large, so you will have more time to focus on more areas. We can cover a lot of ground in an hour and a half, if everyone is participating and paying attention.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: I want to focus on some suggestions about making sales scores, and I was hoping to throw in a few role plays so that people get practise implementing the things I'm going to talk about. Do you think people will go for the role playing?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">F: I think some people may be a little shy to do role playing in front of class… but if you are enthusiastic about your topic, you can help everyone to feel more at ease and willing to give it a try.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don’t put them in the same group. The two of them are at odds with each other.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不要把他们两个分在一个组里，他俩__________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不合</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding:
